SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[CreateDate], [t].[Priority], [t].[Section], [t].[Status], [t].[Title], [t].[UserId]
FROM [Tickets] AS [t]
WHERE [t].[CreateDate] <= DATEADD(day, CAST(-30.0E0 AS int), GETDATE()) AND [t].[Status] <> 3
